        <script>
            var theme = localStorage.getItem('theme');
            var lightToggle = document.querySelector('#theme-light');
            var darkToggle = document.querySelector('#theme-dark');

            if(theme=="dark"){
          	 document.body.setAttribute("data-theme", "dark");
          	 darkToggle.classList.add("more-menu__link--active");
          	 lightToggle.classList.remove("more-menu__link--active");
          	  }

          	if (theme!="light" &amp;&amp; window.matchMedia &amp;&amp; window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches) {
          	document.body.setAttribute("data-theme", "dark");
          	darkToggle.classList.add("more-menu__link--active");
          	lightToggle.classList.remove("more-menu__link--active");
          }
          	window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').addEventListener('change', event =&gt; {
          	  if (event.matches) {
          	document.body.setAttribute("data-theme", "dark");
          	darkToggle.classList.add("more-menu__link--active");
          	lightToggle.classList.remove("more-menu__link--active");
          	localStorage.setItem('theme', 'dark');
            } else {
          	document.body.removeAttribute("data-theme", "dark");
          	lightToggle.classList.add("more-menu__link--active");
          	darkToggle.classList.remove("more-menu__link--active");
          	localStorage.setItem('theme', 'light');
            }
          });
             darkToggle.addEventListener("click", function() {
          	 document.body.setAttribute("data-theme", "dark");
          	 darkToggle.classList.add("more-menu__link--active");
          	 lightToggle.classList.remove("more-menu__link--active");
          	 localStorage.setItem('theme', 'dark');
          	 fathom.trackGoal('6HZLT6XT', 0);
             });

             lightToggle.addEventListener("click", function() {
          	document.body.removeAttribute("data-theme", "dark");
          	lightToggle.classList.add("more-menu__link--active");
          	darkToggle.classList.remove("more-menu__link--active");
          	localStorage.setItem('theme', 'light');
          	fathom.trackGoal('6HZLT6XT', 0);
             });
        </script>
        <script>
          let isCursorLocked = false;
          const cursor = document.getElementById("cursor");
          const cursorContentWrap = document.querySelector(".cursor-content-wrap");
          const cursorContent = document.querySelector(".cursor__content");
          const cursorHighlight = document.querySelector(".cursor-highlight");

          if (window.innerWidth &gt;= 991) {

          document.addEventListener("mousemove", cursorMove);
          function cursorMove(e) {
          	if (!isCursorLocked) {
          		cursor.style.top = e.clientY + "px";
          		cursor.style.left = e.clientX + "px";
          	  }
            cursorHighlight.style.top = e.clientY + "px";
            cursorHighlight.style.left = e.clientX + "px";
            cursorContent.style.opacity = 50 + "%";
          }

          document.addEventListener("mousedown", () =&gt; {
             if (!isCursorLocked) {
          	cursorContentWrap.style.transform = "scale(0.9, 0.9)";
          	cursorContentWrap.style.webkitTransform = "scale(0.9, 0.9)";
          	cursorContent.style.opacity = 80 + "%";
            }
          });

          document.addEventListener("mouseup", () =&gt; {
            if (!isCursorLocked) {
          	cursorContentWrap.style.transform = "scale(1, 1)";
          	cursorContentWrap.style.webkitTransform = "scale(1, 1)";
          	cursorContent.style.opacity = 50 + "%";
            }
          });

          document.querySelectorAll("#a").forEach((a) =&gt; {
            let rect = null;

            a.addEventListener(
          	"mouseenter",
          	({ currentTarget }) =&gt; {
          			if (currentTarget.classList.contains("lift")) {
          				cursorContentWrap.style.opacity = 0 + "%";
          			}
          		  isCursorLocked = true;

          		  rect = currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect();
          		  var targetStyles = window.getComputedStyle(currentTarget);
          		  var targetZIndex = targetStyles.getPropertyValue("z-index");
          		  cursor.classList.add("is-locked");
          		  cursor.style.top = rect.top + rect.height / 2 + "px";
          		  cursor.style.left = rect.left + rect.width / 2 + "px";
          		  cursor.style.width = rect.width + "px";
          		  cursor.style.height = rect.height + "px";
          		  cursorContent.style.borderRadius = 10 + "px";
          		  cursor.style.zIndex = targetZIndex - 1;
          		  cursorHighlight.style.opacity = 30 + "%";
          		  cursorHighlight.style.width = rect.height/2 + "px";
          		  cursorHighlight.style.height = rect.height/2 + "px";
          		  cursorHighlight.style.filter = "blur("+rect.height/4+"px)";
          		  cursorHighlight.style.webkitFilter = "blur("+rect.height/4+"px)";
          	},
          	{ passive: true }
            );

            a.addEventListener(
          	"mousemove",
          	({ currentTarget }) =&gt; {
          	  const halfHeight = rect.height / 2;
          	  const topOffset = (event.y - rect.top - halfHeight) / halfHeight;
          	  const halfWidth = rect.width / 2;
          	  const leftOffset = (event.x - rect.left - halfWidth) / halfWidth;

          		  cursor.style.transform = "translate(" + leftOffset *8 + "px, "+ topOffset *6 +"px)";
          		  cursor.style.webkitTransform = "translate(" + leftOffset *8 + "px, "+ topOffset *6 +"px)";

          		  if (currentTarget.classList.contains("lift")) {

          		  } else {
          			  currentTarget.style.transform = "translate(" + leftOffset *3 +"px, "+ topOffset *2 +"px) scale(1.025, 1.025)";
          			  currentTarget.style.webkitTransform = "translate(" + leftOffset *3 +"px, "+ topOffset *2 +"px) scale(1.025, 1.025)";
          			  }
          	},
          	{ passive: true }
            );

            a.addEventListener(
          	"mouseleave",
          	({ currentTarget }) =&gt; {
          		  isCursorLocked = false;
          		  if (currentTarget.classList.contains("lift")) {
          			  cursorContentWrap.style.opacity = 100 + "%";
          		  }
          		  cursor.style.transitionDuration = 150 + "ms";
          		  cursor.style.width = 20 + "px";
          		  cursor.style.height = 20 + "px";
          		  cursor.style.transform = "translate(0px, 0px)";
          		  currentTarget.style.transform = "translate(0px, 0px) scale(1, 1)";
          		  cursor.style.webkitTransform = "translate(0px, 0px)";
          		  currentTarget.style.webkitTransform = "translate(0px, 0px) scale(1, 1)";
          		  cursor.classList.remove("is-locked");

          		  cursorHighlight.style.opacity = 0 + "%";
          		  cursorHighlight.style.width = 0 + "px";
          		  cursorHighlight.style.height = 0 + "px";
          		  cursorHighlight.style.filter = "blur(0px)";
          		  cursorHighlight.style.webkitFilter = "blur(0px)";

          		  setTimeout(() =&gt; {
          			if (!isCursorLocked) {
          			  cursorContent.style.borderRadius = 50 + "%";
          			  cursor.style.zIndex = 1000;
          			 }
          		  }, 250);
          	},
          	{ passive: true }
            );

            a.addEventListener(
          	  "mousedown",
          	  ({ currentTarget }) =&gt; {
          		cursorContent.style.opacity = 80 + "%";
          	  },
          	  { passive: true }
          	);
          	a.addEventListener(
          		  "mouseup",
          		  ({ currentTarget }) =&gt; {
          			cursorContent.style.opacity = 30 + "%";
          		  },
          		  { passive: true }
          		);
          });
          }
        </script>
        <script>
           document.querySelectorAll('.ix--cta, .faq-front').forEach(trigger =&gt; {

          	document.body.style.overflow = "auto";

          	document.querySelector(".anfrage__success-trigger").click();

          document.querySelector(".anfrage-start-button").addEventListener("click", function() {
          	fathom.trackGoal('AR62WTLP', 0);
             });

          document.querySelectorAll(".more-menu__link.language").forEach(trigger =&gt; {
            trigger.addEventListener('click', function(){
          	sessionStorage.setItem('languageSet', 'true');
            });
          });

        <script>
           class MSF{constructor(t){this.currentStep=0,this.form=document.getElementById(t.formID),this.next=document.getElementById(t.nextButtonID),this.back=document.getElementById(t.backButtonID),this.submitButton=this.form.querySelector('input[type="submit"]'),this.mask=this.form.querySelector(".w-slider-mask"),this.steps=this.form.querySelectorAll(".w-slide"),this.rightArrow=this.form.querySelector(".w-slider-arrow-right"),this.leftArrow=this.form.querySelector(".w-slider-arrow-left"),this.nextText=t.nextButtonText,this.submitText=t.submitButtonText,this.warningClass=t.warningClass,this.alertText=t.alertText,t.alertElementID&amp;&amp;(this.alertElement=document.getElementById(t.alertElementID)),t.hiddenFormID&amp;&amp;(this.hiddenForm=document.getElementById(t.hiddenFormID),this.hiddenSubmitButton=this.hiddenForm.querySelector('input[type="submit"]'))}getInputs(t){const e=this.steps[t].querySelectorAll("input, select, textarea");return Array.from(e)}setMaskHeight(){this.mask.style.height="",this.mask.style.height=`${this.steps[this.currentStep].offsetHeight}px`}setNextButtonText(){this.currentStep===this.steps.length-1&amp;&amp;(this.next.textContent=this.submitText),this.currentStep===this.steps.length-2&amp;&amp;(this.next.textContent=this.nextText)}goNext(){this.rightArrow.click()}goBack(){this.leftArrow.click()}submitForm(){this.submitButton.click()}submitHiddenForm(t){this.getInputs(t).forEach(t=&gt;{const e=document.getElementById(`hidden-${t.id}`);e&amp;&amp;(e.value=t.value)}),this.hiddenSubmitButton.click()}hideButtons(){this.next.style.display="none",this.back.style.display="none"}addWarningClass(t){this.warningClass&amp;&amp;t.classList.add(this.warningClass)}removeWarningClass(t){this.warningClass&amp;&amp;t.classList.remove(this.warningClass)}showAlert(){this.alertText&amp;&amp;alert(this.alertText),this.alertElement&amp;&amp;this.alertElement.classList.remove("hidden")}hideAlert(){this.alertElement&amp;&amp;this.alertElement.classList.add("hidden")}setConfirmValues(t){this.getInputs(t).forEach(t=&gt;{let e,s;if("radio"===t.type){const n=t.getAttribute("name"),i=document.querySelector(`input[name="${n}"]:checked`);i&amp;&amp;(e=i.value,s=document.getElementById(`${n}-value`))}else e=t.value,s=document.getElementById(`${t.id}-value`);e&amp;&amp;s?s.textContent=e:!e&amp;&amp;s&amp;&amp;(s.textContent="-")})}}const msfController={init:t=&gt;{const e=()=&gt;{t.next.addEventListener("click",s),t.back.addEventListener("click",n),t.hiddenForm&amp;&amp;t.rightArrow.addEventListener("click",()=&gt;{t.submitHiddenForm(0)},{once:!0})},s=()=&gt;{i(t.currentStep)?(t.setConfirmValues(t.currentStep),t.currentStep++,t.currentStep===t.steps.length?(t.submitForm(),t.hideButtons(),t.hideAlert()):(t.goNext(),t.setMaskHeight(),t.setNextButtonText(),t.hideAlert())):t.showAlert()},n=()=&gt;{const e=t.currentStep-1;e&gt;=0&amp;&amp;(t.goBack(),t.currentStep=e,t.setMaskHeight(),t.setNextButtonText(),t.hideAlert())},i=e=&gt;{const s=t.getInputs(e).filter(t=&gt;t.required),n=s.filter(t=&gt;"checkbox"===t.type),i=s.filter(t=&gt;"radio"===t.type);let l=0;return s.forEach(e=&gt;{if(e.value&amp;&amp;"email"!==e.type)t.removeWarningClass(e),l++;else if(e.value&amp;&amp;"email"===e.type){r(e.value)?(t.removeWarningClass(e),l++):t.addWarningClass(e)}else t.addWarningClass(e)}),n.forEach(e=&gt;{const s=e.parentNode.querySelector(".w-checkbox-input");e.checked?(s&amp;&amp;t.removeWarningClass(s),l++):s&amp;&amp;t.addWarningClass(s)}),i.forEach(e=&gt;{const s=e.parentNode.querySelector(".w-radio-input"),n=e.getAttribute("name");document.querySelector(`input[name="${n}"]:checked`)?(t.removeWarningClass(s),l++):t.addWarningClass(s)}),l===s.length+n.length+i.length},r=t=&gt;{return/^(([^&lt;&gt;()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^&lt;&gt;()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/.test(String(t).toLowerCase())};e(),t.setMaskHeight(0)}};

           document.getElementById('pageurl').value = url;

        <script>
          var language = navigator.language;
          var supportedLanguages = [

            "de-ch",
            "de-LU",
            "de-lu",
          ];
          var languageSet = sessionStorage.getItem("languageSet");
          if (supportedLanguages.includes(language)) {
            if (!languageSet) {
              document.querySelector(".language-notice-trigger").click();
            }
          } else {
          }
          document
            .querySelector(".language-notice-cancel")
            .addEventListener("click", function () {
              sessionStorage.setItem("languageSet", "true");
            });

          document
            .querySelector(".language-notice-button")
            .addEventListener("click", function () {
              sessionStorage.setItem("languageSet", "true");
            });
        </script>
        <script>
          var Webflow = Webflow || [];
          Webflow.push(function () {
            let msfData = new MSF({
              formID: "projektanfrage",
              nextButtonID: "form-next",
              backButtonID: "form-back",
              nextButtonText: "Next",
              submitButtonText: "Send",
              warningClass: "warning",
            });
            msfController.init(msfData);
          });
        </script>
        <script>
          const projectList = document.querySelectorAll(".projects-list-item");
          const button = document.querySelector(".load-more-button");
          const min = 4;
          const max = projectList.length;
          var visible = min;

          function showUpToIndex(index) {
          		for(var i = 0; i &lt; projectList.length; i++){
          		projectList[i].style.display = "none";
          	}
          	for(var i = 0; i &lt; index; i++){
          		projectList[i].style.display = "block";
          	}
          }

          function disableButton() {
          	if (visible &gt;= max) {
          		visible = max;
          		button.style.display = "none";
          	} else {
          		button.style.display = "inline-block";
          	}
          }
          showUpToIndex(visible);
          disableButton();

          button.onclick = function(e) {
          	e.preventDefault();
          	visible = visible + 2;
          	disableButton();
          	showUpToIndex(visible);
             fathom.trackGoal('SEXGNUP7', 0);
          }
        </script>
        <script>
          document.querySelectorAll('.faq-front').forEach(trigger =&gt; {
            trigger.addEventListener('click', function(){
                this.closest('.faq-item').style.zIndex = 12;
            });
           });

          document.querySelectorAll('.faq-overlay, .faq-back').forEach(trigger =&gt; {
            trigger.addEventListener('click', function(){
                setTimeout(function(){
              document.querySelectorAll('.faq-item').forEach(target =&gt; {
              target.style.zIndex = 1;
              });
               }, 500);
            });
           });
        </script>

        <script
          defer=""
          src="https://unpkg.com/swiper/swiper-bundle.min.js"
        ></script>
        <script>
          var fsmActual = document.createElement('div');
          fsmActual.setAttribute('id', 'fsm_actual');
          document.body.appendChild(fsmActual);
          var $fsm = document.querySelectorAll('.fsm');;
          var $fsmActual = document.querySelector('#fsm_actual');
          $fsmActual.style.position = "absolute";

          var position = {};
          var size = {};

            if (window.innerWidth &gt; 980) {
          	var paddingTop = '64px';
          	var paddingBottom = '64px';
            } else {
          	var paddingTop = '0px';
          	var paddingBottom = '0px';
            }

          var openFSM = function(event) {
          	var $this = event.currentTarget;
          	var clientRect = $this.parentElement.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
          	position = {
          		top: $this.parentElement.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect().top - document.body.getBoundingClientRect().top,
          		left: clientRect.left
          	}

          	size = {
          		width: window.getComputedStyle($this).width,
          		height: window.getComputedStyle($this).height
          	}
          	$fsmActual.style.position = "absolute";
            $fsmActual.style.top = position.top + 'px';
          	$fsmActual.style.left = position.left + 'px';
          	$fsmActual.style.height = size.height;
          	$fsmActual.style.width = size.width;
            $fsmActual.style.margin = $this.style.margin;
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';

          	setTimeout(function(){
          		$fsmActual.innerHTML = $this.innerHTML;
          		var classes = $this.classList.value.split(' ');
          		for (var i = 0; i &lt; classes.length; i++) {
          			$fsmActual.classList.add(classes[i]);
          		}
          		$fsmActual.classList.add('growing');
          		$fsmActual.style.height = '100vh';
          		$fsmActual.style.width = '100%';
          	$fsmActual.style.zIndex = '600';
          	$fsmActual.style.top = window.pageYOffset + 'px';
          		$fsmActual.style.left = '0';
          		$fsmActual.style.margin = '0';
          	$fsmActual.querySelector('.project-item-info-wrap').style.display = 'block';
          	var $fsmClose =  $fsmActual.querySelector('.project-item-close');
          	$fsmClose.addEventListener("click", closeFSM);
          	$fsmActual.style.paddingTop = paddingTop;
          	  $fsmActual.style.paddingBottom = paddingBottom;
          	$fsmActual.querySelector('.project-item-close').style.transform = 'rotate(45deg)';
          	$fsmActual.querySelector('.project-list-item-container').classList.add('opened');
          	$fsmActual.querySelector('.project-item-pause-button').style.opacity = 1;
             $fsmActual.classList.add('opened');
          	}, 0);

          	setTimeout(function(){
          		$fsmActual.classList.remove('growing');
          		$fsmActual.classList.add('full-screen');
          		$fsmActual.querySelector('.project-item-vid').style.opacity = 1;
          		var projectVideo = $fsmActual.querySelector('.project-item-vid video');
          		projectVideo.load();
          		var playPromise = projectVideo.play();
          	  if (playPromise !== undefined) {
          		playPromise.then(_ =&gt; {

          		})
          		.catch(error =&gt; {

          		});
          	  }

               $fsmActual.querySelector('.project-item-pause-button').addEventListener('click', function(){
               	if (this.classList.contains('pause')){
                 	projectVideo.pause();
                   this.querySelector('.project-video-icon--play').style.display = 'block';
                   this.querySelector('.project-video-icon--pause').style.display = 'none';
                   this.classList.remove('pause');
                 } else {
                 	projectVideo.play();
                   this.querySelector('.project-video-icon--play').style.display = 'none';
                   this.querySelector('.project-video-icon--pause').style.display = 'block';
                   this.classList.add('pause');
                 }

               });

          	var swiperElement = $fsmActual.querySelector('.swiper-container');
          	  var swiper = new Swiper(swiperElement, {
          		slidesPerView: 1.8,
          		centeredSlides: true,
          		loop: true,
          		spaceBetween: 64,
          		speed: 800,
          		lazyLoading: true,
          		autoplay: {
          				   delay: 2000,
                      disableOnInteraction: false,
          				 },
          	  });
          	}, 500);
          };

          var closeFSM = function(event){
          	var $this = $fsmActual;

          	$this.style.height = size.height;
          	$this.style.width = size.width;
          	$this.style.top = position.top + 'px';
          	$this.style.left = position.left + 'px';
          	$this.style.margin = '0';
          	$this.classList.remove('full-screen');
          	$this.classList.add('shrinking');
            $fsmActual.style.paddingTop = '0px';
            document.querySelector('.project-overlay-close-trigger').click();
            document.body.style.overflow = 'auto';
            $fsmActual.querySelector('.project-item-close').style.transform = 'rotate(0deg)';
            $fsmActual.querySelector('.project-list-item-container').classList.remove('opened');
            $fsmActual.classList.remove('opened');
            $fsmActual.querySelector('.project-item-vid video').pause();
            $fsmActual.querySelector('.project-item-vid').style.opacity = 0;
             $fsmActual.querySelector('.project-item-pause-button').style.opacity = 0;

          	setTimeout(function(){
          		while($this.firstChild) $this.removeChild($this.firstChild);
          		var classList = $this.classList;
          		while (classList.length &gt; 0) {
          			 classList.remove(classList.item(0));
          		}
          		$this.style = '';;
          	}, 500);
          };

          for (var i = 0; i &lt; $fsm.length; i++) {
          	$fsm[i].addEventListener("click", openFSM);
          }
        </script>
        <div id="fsm_actual" style="position: absolute"></div>
        <script>
          document.querySelectorAll('.projects-list-item').forEach(trigger =&gt; {
          	  trigger.addEventListener('click', function(){
          		var fathomID = this.querySelector('#fathom-id').innerHTML;
          		fathom.trackGoal(fathomID, 0);
          	  });
          	 });
        </script>
      </body>
